_MISC:Button('Universal Teleport Menu (OP)', function()

    _ScreenGui.Name = 'PlayerButtonsGui'
    _ScreenGui.Parent = game:GetService('CoreGui')

    local _Frame = Instance.new('Frame')

    _Frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 300, 0, 400)
    _Frame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10)
    _Frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(53, 53, 53)
    _Frame.BorderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(34, 34, 34)
    _Frame.Active = true
    _Frame.Draggable = true
    _Frame.Parent = _ScreenGui

    local _TextButton = Instance.new('TextButton')

    _TextButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20)
    _TextButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 5, 0, 5)
    _TextButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
    _TextButton.Text = 'X'
    _TextButton.Parent = _Frame

    local _TextButton2 = Instance.new('TextButton')

    _TextButton2.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20)
    _TextButton2.Position = UDim2.new(1, -25, 0, 5)
    _TextButton2.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 102, 102)
    _TextButton2.Text = '-'
    _TextButton2.Parent = _Frame

    local _ScrollingFrame = Instance.new('ScrollingFrame')

    _ScrollingFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 1, -30)
    _ScrollingFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 5, 0, 25)
    _ScrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
    _ScrollingFrame.Parent = _Frame
    _ScrollingFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1

    local function u79(p78)
        _LocalPlayer4.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = p78.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
    end
    local function u86(p80)
        local _TextButton3 = Instance.new('TextButton')

        _TextButton3.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)

        local v82 = _ScrollingFrame

        _TextButton3.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, #v82:GetChildren() * 40)
        _TextButton3.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(34, 139, 34)
        _TextButton3.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        _TextButton3.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        _TextButton3.TextSize = 12
        _TextButton3.Text = p80.Name
        _TextButton3.TextWrapped = true
        _TextButton3.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        _TextButton3.Parent = _ScrollingFrame

        local _TextButton4 = Instance.new('TextButton')

        _TextButton4.Size = UDim2.new(0.5, -5, 1, 0)
        _TextButton4.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 5, 0, 0)
        _TextButton4.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(139, 34, 34)
        _TextButton4.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        _TextButton4.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        _TextButton4.TextSize = 10
        _TextButton4.Text = 'Loop TP'
        _TextButton4.TextWrapped = true
        _TextButton4.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
        _TextButton4.Parent = _TextButton3

        local u84 = false
        local u85 = nil

        _TextButton4.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if u84 then
                _TextButton4.Text = 'Loop TP'

                u85:Disconnect()

                u84 = false
            else
                _TextButton4.Text = 'Stop TP'
                u85 = _RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
                    if _LocalPlayer4.Character and p80.Character then
                        u79(p80)
                    end
                end)
                u84 = true
            end
        end)
        _TextButton3.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if not u84 then
                u79(p80)
            end
        end)
    end

    local v87, v88, v89 = ipairs(_Players3:GetPlayers())
    local u90 = _ScrollingFrame
    local v91 = _LocalPlayer4

    while true do
        local v92

        v89, v92 = v87(v88, v89)

        if v89 == nil then
            break
        end
        if v92 ~= v91 then
            u86(v92)
        end
    end

    _Players3.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(p93)
        u86(p93)
    end)
    _Players3.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(p94)
        local v95 = u90:GetChildren()
        local v96, v97, v98 = ipairs(v95)

        while true do
            local v99

            v98, v99 = v96(v97, v98)

            if v98 == nil then
                break
            end
            if v99:IsA('TextButton') and v99.Text == p94.Name then
                v99:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end)
    _TextButton2.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if _Frame.Size ~= UDim2.new(0, 300, 0, 400) then
            _Frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 300, 0, 400)
            _TextButton2.Text = '-'
            _TextButton2.Position = UDim2.new(1, -25, 0, 5)
        else
            _Frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 30)
            _TextButton2.Text = '+'
            _TextButton2.Position = UDim2.new(1, -25, 0, 5)
        end
    end)
    _TextButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        _ScreenGui:Destroy()
    end)
    u1:Notification('Notification', 'Universal Teleport Menu (OP)', 'Okay!')
end)

    function GetSpeed()

            local _SpeedBoost = _LocalPlayer5.Character:GetAttribute('SpeedBoost')

            if _SpeedBoost and 1 < _SpeedBoost then
                v480 = v480 + 20 * (_SpeedBoost - 1)
            end
            if _LocalPlayer5.Character:GetAttribute('SpeedPieBuff') then
                v480 = v480 + 5
            end
            if _LocalPlayer5.Character:GetAttribute('GrimReaperChannel') then
                v480 = v480 + 20
            end
            if u284 ~= 0 then
                v480 = v480 + 19
            end
            if u282 == true then
                v480 = v480 + 18
            end
            if u276 == true then
                v480 = v480 + 19
            end

            v480 = v480 + u234.Speed.Speed - 20
        end

        return v480
    end

_LocksCamlocks:Button('Enable Slapware AUTO PING (OP)', function()
    getgenv().Prediction = 0.1248710929171
    getgenv().AimPart = 'HumanoidRootPart'
    getgenv().Key = 'Q'
    getgenv().DisableKey = 'P'
    getgenv().FOV = true
    getgenv().ShowFOV = false
    getgenv().FOVSize = 55

    local _Players5 = game:GetService('Players')
    local _RunService3 = game:GetService('RunService')
    local _Workspace = game:GetService('Workspace')
    local _GuiService = game:GetService('GuiService')
    local _StarterGui3 = game:GetService('StarterGui')
    local u1225 = _Players5.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
    local _CurrentCamera3 = _Workspace.CurrentCamera
    local _GetGuiInset = _GuiService.GetGuiInset
    local u1228 = true
    local u1229 = nil
    local u1230 = nil
    local _Key = getgenv().Key
    local _DisableKey = getgenv().DisableKey

    function Notify(p1233)
        _StarterGui3:SetCore('SendNotification', {
            Title = 'SLAPWARE (update)',
            Text = p1233,
            Duration = 5,
        })
    end

    if getgenv().Loaded ~= true then
        getgenv().Loaded = true

        local _Circle = Drawing.new('Circle')

        _Circle.Filled = false
        _Circle.Transparency = 1
        _Circle.Thickness = 1
        _Circle.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0)
        _Circle.NumSides = 1000

        function update()
            if getgenv().FOV == true and _Circle then
                _Circle.Radius = getgenv().FOVSize * 2
                _Circle.Visible = getgenv().ShowFOV
                _Circle.Position = Vector2.new(u1225.X, u1225.Y + _GetGuiInset(_GuiService).Y)

                return _Circle
            end
        end
        function WTVP(p1235)
            return _CurrentCamera3:WorldToViewportPoint(p1235)
        end
        function WTSP(p1236)
            return _CurrentCamera3:WorldToScreenPoint(p1236)
        end
        function getClosest()
            local _huge7 = math.huge
            local v1238, v1239, v1240 = pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())
            local v1241 = nil

            while true do
                local v1242

                v1240, v1242 = v1238(v1239, v1240)

                if v1240 == nil then
                    break
                end

                local v1243 = v1242.Character:WaitForChild('BodyEffects')['K.O'].Value ~= true
                local v1244 = v1242.Character:FindFirstChild('GRABBING_COINSTRAINT') == nil

                if v1242 ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and v1242.Character and (v1242.Character:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and v1242.Character.Humanoid.Health ~= 0 and (v1242.Character:FindFirstChild(getgenv().AimPart) and (v1243 and v1244))) then
                    local v1245 = _CurrentCamera3:WorldToViewportPoint(v1242.Character.PrimaryPart.Position)
                    local _magnitude6 = (Vector2.new(v1245.X, v1245.Y) - Vector2.new(u1225.X, u1225.Y)).magnitude

                    if getgenv().FOV then
                        if _magnitude6 < _Circle.Radius then
                            if _magnitude6 < _huge7 then
                                v1241 = v1242
                                _huge7 = _magnitude6
                            end
                        end
                    elseif _magnitude6 < _huge7 then
                        v1241 = v1242
                        _huge7 = _magnitude6
                    end
                end
            end

            return v1241
        end

        u1225.KeyDown:Connect(function(p1247)
            _Key = _Key:lower()
            _DisableKey = _DisableKey:lower()

            if p1247 == _Key then
                if u1228 ~= true then
                    Notify('Aimlock is not enabled!')
                else
                    u1229 = not u1229

                    if u1229 then
                        u1230 = getClosest()

                        Notify('Locked onto: ' .. tostring(u1230.Character.Humanoid.DisplayName))
                    elseif u1230 ~= nil then
                        u1230 = nil

                        Notify('Unlocked!')
                    end
                end
            end
            if p1247 == _DisableKey then
                u1228 = not u1228
            end
        end)
        _RunService3.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
            update()

            if u1228 == true and u1230 ~= nil then
                _CurrentCamera3.CFrame = CFrame.new(_CurrentCamera3.CFrame.p, u1230.Character[getgenv().AimPart].Position + u1230.Character[getgenv().AimPart].Velocity * getgenv().Prediction)
            end
        end)

        while wait() do
            if getgenv().AutoPrediction == true then
                local v1248 = game:GetService('Stats').Network.ServerStatsItem['Data Ping']:GetValueString()
                local v1249 = string.split(v1248, '(')
                local v1250 = tonumber(v1249[1])

                if v1250 < 225 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 1.4
                elseif v1250 < 215 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 1.2
                elseif v1250 < 205 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 1
                elseif v1250 < 190 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.1
                elseif v1250 < 180 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.12
                elseif v1250 < 170 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.15
                elseif v1250 < 160 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.18
                elseif v1250 < 150 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.11
                elseif v1250 < 140 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.113
                elseif v1250 < 130 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.116
                elseif v1250 < 120 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.12
                elseif v1250 < 110 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.124
                elseif v1250 < 105 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.127
                elseif v1250 < 90 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.13
                elseif v1250 < 80 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.133
                elseif v1250 < 70 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.136
                elseif v1250 < 60 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.14
                elseif v1250 < 50 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.143
                elseif v1250 < 40 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.145
                elseif v1250 < 30 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.155
                elseif v1250 < 20 then
                    getgenv().Prediction = 0.157
                end
            end
        end

        u1:Notification('Notification', 'Slapware Activated', 'Okay!')
    else
        Notify('Aimlock is already loaded!')
    end
end)

    function stepped()
        pcall(function()
            if _LocalPlayer20.Character and (_LocalPlayer20.Character:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and _G.Aimbot) then
                power()

                local v1780, _ = setup()
                local _HumanoidRootPart4 = _LocalPlayer20.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                local v1782 = math.floor(v1780)

                if _HumanoidRootPart4 and hasBall then
                    _HumanoidRootPart4.Size = Vector3.new(2.1, 2.1, 1.1)
                    _HumanoidRootPart4.BrickColor = BrickColor.new('Lime green')
                    _HumanoidRootPart4.Material = Enum.Material.Neon

                    if 13 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 16 then
                        changePower(30)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 17 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 21 then
                        changePower(35)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 22 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 26 then
                        changePower(40)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 27 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 31 then
                        changePower(45)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 32 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 36 then
                        changePower(50)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 37 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 41 then
                        changePower(55)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 42 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 46 then
                        changePower(60)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 47 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 50 then
                        changePower(65)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 51 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 56 then
                        changePower(70)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 57 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 61 then
                        changePower(75)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 62 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 67 then
                        changePower(80)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif 68 <= v1782 and v1782 <= 74 then
                        changePower(85)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    elseif u1725 and v1782 == 9 or (v1782 == 10 or (v1782 == 11 or v1782 == 12)) then
                        changePower(25)

                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 0
                    else
                        _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 1
                    end
                elseif _HumanoidRootPart4 and (not hasBall and _G.Aimbot) then
                    _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 1
                elseif _HumanoidRootPart4 and not _G.Aimbot then
                    _HumanoidRootPart4.Transparency = 1
                end
            end

            updateNearestPlayerWithBall()

            if _G.WS ~= 16 and _LocalPlayer20.Character:WaitForChild('Humanoid').WalkSpeed ~= 0 then
                _LocalPlayer20.Character:WaitForChild('Humanoid').WalkSpeed = _G.WS
            end
            if _G.Autogaurd and (u1748 and (u1749 and _LocalPlayer20.Character)) and (_LocalPlayer20.Character:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and (not _LocalPlayer20.Character:FindFirstChild('Basketball') and u1749.Character and u1749.Character:FindFirstChild('Basketball'))) then
                _LocalPlayer20.Character.Humanoid:MoveTo(u1749.Character.Basketball:FindFirstChildOfClass('Part').Position + u1749.Character.Torso.CFrame.LookVector + (u1749.Character.Humanoid.MoveDirection * 2 + _LocalPlayer20.Character.Torso.Velocity.Unit * 3))

                if u1749.Character.Torso.Position.Y - u1747.Position.Y > 2.5 then
                    _LocalPlayer20.Character.Humanoid.Jump = true
                end
            elseif u1748 and (u1749 ~= nil and (u1749.Character and _LocalPlayer20.Character)) and _LocalPlayer20.Character:FindFirstChild('Basketball') or not u1749.Character:FindFirstChild('Basketball') then
                u1748 = false

                return
            end

            local v1783, v1784, v1785 = pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())

            while true do
                local v1786

                v1785, v1786 = v1783(v1784, v1785)

                if v1785 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v1786.Name ~= _LocalPlayer20.Name and (v1786.Character and (_LocalPlayer20.Character and _G.Reach)) then
                    local v1787 = getNearestPart(v1786.Character.Torso)
                    local v1788, v1789, v1790 = pairs(v1786.Character:GetChildren())

                    while true do
                        local v1791

                        v1790, v1791 = v1788(v1789, v1790)

                        if v1790 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if (v1787.Position - v1786.Character.Torso.Position).Magnitude < 8 then
                            if v1791:IsA('Tool') or v1791:IsA('Folder') then
                                firetouchinterest(v1787, v1791:FindFirstChildOfClass('Part'), 0)
                                task.wait()

                                task.wait()
                                firetouchinterest(v1787, v1791, 1)
                            end
                        end

                end
            end
        end)
    end
